dao package

 

IBookDAO.java

package dao;

import java.util.List;

import Book;

public interface IBookDAO {

public boolean doCreate(Book book)throws Exception;

public boolean doUpdate(Book book)throws Exception;

public boolean doDelete(String id)throws Exception;

public Book findById(String id)throws Exception;

public List<Book> findAll(String keyword)throws Exception;

}

dao.dbc Package

DataBaseConnection.java

package dao.dbc;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.DriverManager;
import java.sql.SQLException;

public class DataBaseConnection {

private static final String DBDRIVER="com.mysql.jdbc.Driver";
private static final String DBURL="jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/_library";
private static final String DBUSER="root";
private static final String DBPASS="rain";
private Connection conn=null;

public DataBaseConnection(){
try {
Class.forName(DBDRIVER);
} catch (ClassNotFoundException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
try {
conn=DriverManager.getConnection(DBURL, DBUSER, DBPASS);
} catch (SQLException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
public Connection getConnection(){
return this.conn;
}
public void close(){
if(this.conn!=null){
try {
this.conn.close();
} catch (SQLException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
}
}

dao.impl package

IBookDAOImpl.java

package dao.impl;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import com.agen.library.dao.IBookDAO;
import com.agen.library.vo.Book;


public class IBookDAOImpl implements IBookDAO {
private Connection conn=null;
public IBookDAOImpl(Connection conn){
this.conn=conn;
}
@Override
public boolean doCreate(Book book) throws Exception {

boolean flag=false;
PreparedStatement pstmt=null;
String sql="INSERT INTO library_book(id,name,author,classify,price,news,publishdata)VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)";
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, book.getId());
pstmt.setString(2, book.getName());
pstmt.setString(3, book.getAuthor());
pstmt.setString(4,book.getClassify());
pstmt.setDouble(5, book.getPrice());
pstmt.setString(6,book.getNews());
pstmt.setDate(7, new java.sql.Date(book.getPublishdata().getTime()));
if(pstmt.executeUpdate()>0){
flag=true;
}
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doDelete(String id) throws Exception {
//¨¦?3y¨ª?¨º¨¦D??¡é
boolean flag=false;
PreparedStatement pstmt=null;
String sql="DELETE FROM library_book WHERE id=?";
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, id);
if(pstmt.executeUpdate()>0){
flag=true;
}
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}

return flag;

}

@Override
public boolean doUpdate(Book book) throws Exception {
// ?¨¹D?¨ª?¨º¨¦D??¡é
boolean flag=false;
PreparedStatement pstmt=null;
String sql="UPDATE library_book SET name=?,author=?,classify=?,price=?,news=?,publishdata=? WHERE id=?";
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, book.getName());
pstmt.setString(2, book.getAuthor());
pstmt.setString(3,book.getClassify());
pstmt.setDouble(4, book.getPrice());
pstmt.setString(5,book.getNews());
pstmt.setDate(6, new java.sql.Date(book.getPublishdata().getTime()));
pstmt.setString(7,book.getId());
if(pstmt.executeUpdate()>0){
flag=true;
}
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public List<Book> findAll(String keyword) throws Exception {
// 2¨¦?¨°¨ª?¨º¨¦D??¡é---1??¨¹¡Á?2¨¦?¨°
List<Book> all=new ArrayList<Book>();
PreparedStatement pstmt=null;
String sql="SELECT incre_id,id,name,author,classify,price,news,publishdata FROM library_book where id LIKE ? OR name LIKE ? OR author LIKE ? OR classify LIKE ? " ;
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(2, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(3, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(4, "%"+keyword+"%");
ResultSet rs=pstmt.executeQuery();
while(rs.next()){
Book book=new Book();
book.setIncre_id(rs.getInt(1));
book.setId(rs.getString(2));
book.setName(rs.getString(3));
book.setAuthor(rs.getString(4));
book.setClassify(rs.getString(5));
book.setPrice(rs.getDouble(6));
book.setNews(rs.getString(7));
book.setPublishdata(rs.getDate(8));
all.add(book);
}
rs.close();
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}
return all;
}

@Override
public Book findById(String id) throws Exception {

Book book = null;
PreparedStatement pstmt=null;
String sql="SELECT incre_id,id,name,author,classify,price,news,publishdata FROM library_book WHERE id=?";
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, id);
ResultSet rs=pstmt.executeQuery();
while(rs.next()){
book =new Book();
book.setIncre_id(rs.getInt(1));
book.setId(rs.getString(2));
book.setName(rs.getString(3));
book.setAuthor(rs.getString(4));
book.setClassify(rs.getString(5));
book.setPrice(rs.getDouble(6));
book.setNews(rs.getString(7));
book.setPublishdata(rs.getDate(8));
}
rs.close();
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}
return book;
}

}

 

IBorrowDAOImpl.java

package dao.impl;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import com.agen.library.dao.IBorrowDAO;
import com.agen.library.vo.Borrow;


public class IBorrowDAOImpl implements IBorrowDAO {
private Connection conn = null;
public IBorrowDAOImpl(Connection conn) {
this.conn = conn;
}

@Override
public boolean doCreate(Borrow borrow) throws Exception {
//???¨®?¨¨??D??¡é
boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "INSERT INTO library_borrow(book_id,reader_id ,borrow_date,back_date,is_back)VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, borrow.getBook_id());
pstmt.setString(2, borrow.getReader_id());
pstmt.setDate(3, new java.sql.Date(borrow.getBorrow_date()
.getTime()));
pstmt.setDate(4, new java.sql.Date(borrow.getBack_date().getTime()));
pstmt.setInt(5, borrow.getIs_back());
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doUpdate(Borrow borrow) throws Exception {

boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "UPDATE library_borrow SET book_id=?,borrow_date=?,back_date=?,is_back=? WHERE reader_id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, borrow.getBook_id());
pstmt.setDate(2, new java.sql.Date(borrow.getBorrow_date().getTime()));
pstmt.setDate(3, new java.sql.Date(borrow.getBack_date().getTime()));
pstmt.setInt(4, borrow.getIs_back());
pstmt.setString(5, borrow.getReader_id());
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doDelete(int id) throws Exception {

boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "DELETE FROM library_borrow WHERE id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setInt(1, id);
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public Borrow findById(String id) throws Exception {

Borrow borrow = null;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "SELECT * FROM library_borrow WHERE reader_id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, id);
ResultSet rs = pstmt.executeQuery();
while (rs.next()) {
borrow = new Borrow();
borrow.setId(rs.getInt(1));
borrow.setReader_id(rs.getString(2));
borrow.setBook_id(rs.getString(3));
borrow.setBorrow_date(rs.getDate(4));
borrow.setBack_date(rs.getDate(5));
borrow.setIs_back(rs.getInt(6));
}
rs.close();
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}
return borrow;
}

@Override
public Borrow findById(int id) throws Exception {

Borrow borrow = null;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "SELECT * FROM library_borrow WHERE id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setInt(1, id);
ResultSet rs = pstmt.executeQuery();
while (rs.next()) {
borrow = new Borrow();
borrow.setId(rs.getInt(1));
borrow.setReader_id(rs.getString(2));
borrow.setBook_id(rs.getString(3));
borrow.setBorrow_date(rs.getDate(4));
borrow.setBack_date(rs.getDate(5));
borrow.setIs_back(rs.getInt(6));
}
rs.close();
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}
return borrow;
}

@Override
public List<Borrow> findAll(String keyword) throws Exception {

List<Borrow> all=new ArrayList<Borrow>();
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql="SELECT id,reader_id,book_id,borrow_date,back_date,is_back FROM library_borrow WHERE reader_id LIKE ? OR book_id LIKE ? OR borrow_date LIKE ? OR back_date LIKE ? OR is_back LIKE ?";
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(2, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(3, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(4, "%"+keyword+"%");
pstmt.setString(5, "%"+keyword+"%");
ResultSet rs=pstmt.executeQuery();
while(rs.next()){
Borrow borrow = new Borrow();
borrow.setId(rs.getInt(1));
borrow.setReader_id(rs.getString(2));
borrow.setBook_id(rs.getString(3));
borrow.setBorrow_date(rs.getDate(4));
borrow.setBack_date(rs.getDate(5));
borrow.setIs_back(rs.getInt(6));
all.add(borrow);
}
rs.close();
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}
return all;
}

}


IReaderDAOImpl.java

package dao.impl;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import com.agen.library.dao.IReaderDAO;
import com.agen.library.vo.Reader;


public class IReaderDAOImpl implements IReaderDAO {
private Connection conn=null;
public IReaderDAOImpl(Connection conn){
this.conn=conn;
}

@Override
public boolean doCreate(Reader reader) throws Exception {

boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "INSERT INTO library_reader(id,name ,type,sex,days_num)VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, reader.getId());
pstmt.setString(2, reader.getName());
pstmt.setString(3, reader.getType());
pstmt.setString(4, reader.getSex());
pstmt.setInt(5, reader.getDays_num());
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

IUserDAOImpl.java

package dao.impl;

import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import com.agen.library.dao.IUserDAO;
import com.agen.library.vo.User;


public class IUserDAOImpl implements IUserDAO {
private Connection conn=null;
public IUserDAOImpl(Connection conn){
this.conn=conn;
}
@Override
public boolean doCreate(User user) throws Exception {

boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "INSERT INTO library_user(login_id,name ,pass,is_admin)VALUES(?,?,?,?)";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, user.getLogin_id());
pstmt.setString(2, user.getName());
pstmt.setString(3, user.getPass());
pstmt.setInt(4, user.getIs_admin());
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doUpdate(User user) throws Exception {

boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "UPDATE library_user SET pass=?,is_admin=? WHERE login_id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, user.getPass());
pstmt.setInt(2, user.getIs_admin());
pstmt.setString(3,user.getLogin_id());
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doDelete(String id) throws Exception {

boolean flag = false;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "DELETE FROM library_user WHERE login_id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, id);
if (pstmt.executeUpdate() > 0) {
flag = true;
}
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}

return flag;
}

@Override
public User findById(String id) throws Exception {

User user = null;
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql = "SELECT * FROM library_user WHERE login_id=?";
try {
pstmt = this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, id);
ResultSet rs = pstmt.executeQuery();
while (rs.next()) {
user = new User();
user.setId(rs.getInt(1));
user.setLogin_id(rs.getString(2));
user.setName(rs.getString(3));
user.setPass(rs.getString(4));
user.setIs_admin(rs.getInt(5));
}
rs.close();
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
try {
if (pstmt != null) {
pstmt.close();
}

} catch (Exception e) {
}
}
return user;
}

@Override
public List<User> findAll(String keyword) throws Exception {

List<User> all=new ArrayList<User>();
PreparedStatement pstmt = null;
String sql="SELECT id,login_id,name,pass,is_admin FROM library_user WHERE name LIKE ? OR login_id LIKE ?";
try{
pstmt=this.conn.prepareStatement(sql);
pstmt.setString(1, "%" + keyword + "%");
pstmt.setString(2, "%"+keyword+"%");
ResultSet rs=pstmt.executeQuery();
while(rs.next()){
User user = new User();
user.setId(rs.getInt(1));
user.setLogin_id(rs.getString(2));
user.setName(rs.getString(3));
user.setPass(rs.getString(4));
user.setIs_admin(rs.getInt(5));
all.add(user);
}
rs.close();
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
try{
if(pstmt!=null){
pstmt.close();
}

}catch(Exception e){}
}
return all;
}

}

dao.proxy package

IBookDAOImplProxy.java

package dao.proxy;

import java.util.List;

import com.agen.library.dao.IBookDAO;
import com.agen.library.dao.dbc.DataBaseConnection;
import com.agen.library.dao.impl.IBookDAOImpl;
import com.agen.library.vo.Book;


public class IBookDAOImplProxy implements IBookDAO {
private IBookDAO dao=null;
private DataBaseConnection dbc=null;
public IBookDAOImplProxy(){
this.dbc=new DataBaseConnection();
this.dao=new IBookDAOImpl(this.dbc.getConnection());
}
@Override
public boolean doCreate(Book book) throws Exception {

boolean flag=true;
try{
flag=this.dao.doCreate(book);
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
this.dbc.close();
}
return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doDelete(String id) throws Exception {

boolean flag=true;
try{
flag=this.dao.doDelete(id);
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
this.dbc.close();
}
return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doUpdate(Book book) throws Exception {

boolean flag=true;
try{
flag=this.dao.doUpdate(book);
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
this.dbc.close();
}
return flag;
}

@Override
public List<Book> findAll(String keyword) throws Exception {

List<Book> all=null;
try{
all=this.dao.findAll(keyword);
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
this.dbc.close();
}
return all;
}

@Override
public Book findById(String id) throws Exception {

Book book=null;
try{
book=this.dao.findById(id);
}catch(Exception e){
throw e;
}finally{
this.dbc.close();
}
return book;
}

}

IBorrowDAOImplProxy.java

package dao.proxy;

import java.util.List;

import com.agen.library.dao.IBorrowDAO;
import com.agen.library.dao.dbc.DataBaseConnection;
import com.agen.library.dao.impl.IBorrowDAOImpl;
import com.agen.library.vo.Borrow;


public class IBorrowDAOImplProxy implements IBorrowDAO {
private DataBaseConnection dbc = null;
private IBorrowDAO dao = null;

public IBorrowDAOImplProxy() {
this.dbc = new DataBaseConnection();
this.dao = new IBorrowDAOImpl(this.dbc.getConnection());
}

@Override
public boolean doCreate(Borrow borrow) throws Exception {

boolean flag = true;
try {
flag = this.dao.doCreate(borrow);
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
this.dbc.close();
}
return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doUpdate(Borrow borrow) throws Exception {

boolean flag = true;
try {
flag = this.dao.doUpdate(borrow);
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
this.dbc.close();
}
return flag;
}

@Override
public boolean doDelete(int id) throws Exception {

boolean flag = true;
try {
flag = this.dao.doDelete(id);
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
this.dbc.close();
}
return flag;
}

@Override
public Borrow findById(String id) throws Exception {

Borrow borrow = null;
try {
borrow = this.dao.findById(id);
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
this.dbc.close();
}
return borrow;
}

@Override
public Borrow findById(int id) throws Exception {

Borrow borrow = null;
try {
borrow = this.dao.findById(id);
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
this.dbc.close();
}
return borrow;
}

@Override
public List<Borrow> findAll(String keyword) throws Exception {

List<Borrow> all = null;
try {
all = this.dao.findAll(keyword);
} catch (Exception e) {
throw e;
} finally {
this.dbc.close();
}
return all;
}

}

util package

DateUtil.java

package util;

import java.text.ParseException;
import java.text.SimpleDateFormat;
import java.util.Calendar;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.Locale;

public class DateUtil {

public static String getAfterDay(String date, int num) {
SimpleDateFormat parser = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd");
Date dt = null;
try {
dt = parser.parse(date);
} catch (ParseException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}

Calendar calendar = Calendar.getInstance();
calendar.setTime(dt);
calendar.add(Calendar.DATE, num);
SimpleDateFormat simpledateformat = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd",
Locale.ENGLISH);
return simpledateformat.format(calendar.getTime());
}

public static String getBeforeDate(int num) {
Calendar calendar = Calendar.getInstance();
calendar.setTime(new Date());
calendar.add(Calendar.DATE, -num);
SimpleDateFormat simpledateformat = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd",
Locale.ENGLISH);
return simpledateformat.format(calendar.getTime());
}

public static String getDate() {
Date dt = new Date();
long tmLong = dt.getTime();
return (new java.sql.Date(tmLong)).toString();
}

public static String getDateTime() {
Date dt = new Date();
Long tmLong = dt.getTime();
return (new java.sql.Date(tmLong) + " " + (new java.sql.Time(tmLong)))
.toString();

}

public static java.sql.Date getStringToDate(String day) {
SimpleDateFormat parser = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd");
Date dt = new Date();
try {
dt = parser.parse(day);
} catch (ParseException e) {
e.printStackTrace();
}
return (new java.sql.Date(dt.getTime()));
}

}

"Java Runtime environment suppliers: "+System.getProperty("java.vendor")+"\n"+"Java supplier's URL: "+System.getProperty("java.vendor.url")+"\n"+
"Java The specification version of virtual machine:"+System.getProperty("java.vm.specification.version")+"\n"+"Java java.class.path:"+System.getProperty("java.class.path")+
"\n"+"The name of the operating system: "+System.getProperty("os.name")+"\n"+"The framework of the operating system: "+System.getProperty("os.arch")+"\n"+
"The version of the operating system: "+System.getProperty("os.version")+"\n"+"The account name of the user: "+System.getProperty("user.name")+"\n"+
"The current working directory of users:"+System.getProperty("user.dir");

package vo;

import java.util.Date;

public class Book {
private int incre_id;
private String author;
private String classify;
private String id;
private String name;
private String news;
private double price;
private Date publishdata;

 

public String getClassify() {
return classify;
}

public String getId() {
return id;
}

public String getName() {
return name;
}

public String getNews() {
return news;
}

public double getPrice() {
return price;
}

public Date getPublishdata() {
return publishdata;
}

public String getAuthor() {
return author;
}

public void setAuthor(String author) {
this.author = author;
}

public void setClassify(String classify) {
this.classify = classify;
}

public void setId(String id) {
this.id = id;
}

public void setName(String name) {
this.name = name;
}

public void setNews(String news) {
this.news = news;
}

public void setPrice(double price) {
this.price = price;
}

public void setPublishdata(Date publishdata) {
this.publishdata = publishdata;
}
public int getIncre_id() {
return incre_id;
}

public void setIncre_id(int incre_id) {
this.incre_id = incre_id;
}


@Override
public String toString() {
return "\n"+"running number¡êo"+incre_id+"\n\n"+"serial number:"+id+"\n\n"+"book name¡êo"+name+"\n\n"+"author¡êo"+author+
"\n\n"+"category¡êo"+classify+"\n\n"+"price¡êo"+price+"\n\n"+"publish date¡êo"+publishdata+
"\n\n"+"abstract¡êo"+news;
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
this.dispose();

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
//DT???¨¹??
String pass = String.valueOf(jPasswordField1.getPassword());
String new_pass = String.valueOf(jPasswordField2.getPassword());
String config_pass = String.valueOf(jPasswordField3.getPassword());

if (pass != null && !pass.equals("") && new_pass != null
&& !new_pass.equals("") && config_pass != null
&& !config_pass.equals("")) {
String old_pass = GlobalUser.LOGIN_USER.getPass();
if (pass.equals(old_pass)) {

if (new_pass.equals(config_pass)) {

GlobalUser.LOGIN_USER.setPass(new_pass);
boolean flag = false;
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().doUpdate(
GlobalUser.LOGIN_USER);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "modification success", "message", 1);
} else {
return;
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Two password is not consistent, please enter again¡ê?", "message",
2);
}

} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "password wrong¡ê?", "message", 2);
return;
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "please enter the password¡ê?", "message", 2);
}

}

private void jTextField1KeyPressed(java.awt.event.KeyEvent evt) {

if (evt.getKeyChar() == '\n') {
jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("Searching...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<Book> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(results,
head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { false,true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("Query Done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);

new Thread() {
public void run() {
int i = 0;
while (i <= need_time) {
try {
Thread.sleep(1);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
}

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {

jProgressBar1.setValue(100);
jLabel2.setText("Query Done");
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding information", "message", 1);
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
return;
}

}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);

//¨¦¨¨??¡Á¡ä¨¬?
Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("Searching...");

//?¨®¨º?1??¨¹¡Á?
String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<Book> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size()!= 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(results,
head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] {false, true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("Query Done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);

new Thread() {
public void run() {

private void jTextField1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// TODO add your handling code here:
}

private Object[][] getResult(List<Book> list) {
Object[][] results = new Object[list.size()][head.length];
for (int i = 0; i < list.size(); i++) {
Book book = list.get(i);
results[i][0] = book.getIncre_id();
results[i][1] = book.getId();
results[i][2] = book.getName();
results[i][3] = book.getAuthor();
results[i][4] = book.getClassify();
results[i][5] = book.getPrice();
results[i][6] = book.getPublishdata();
results[i][7] = book.getNews();
}
return results;
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
String id = jTextField1.getText().trim();
String name = jTextField2.getText().trim();
String author = jTextField3.getText();
String classify = (String) jComboBox1.getSelectedItem();
String price = jTextField5.getText().trim();
String publishdata = jTextField6.getText().trim();
String news = jTextArea1.getText().trim();
Book book = new Book();
book.setId(id);
book.setName(name);
book.setAuthor(author);
book.setClassify(classify);
book.setPrice(Double.parseDouble(price));
book.setNews(news);
book.setPublishdata(DateUtil.getStringToDate(publishdata));
boolean flag = false;
if (book != null) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().doCreate(book);
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Add successful", "message", 1);

}
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
}

}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// 2¨¦?¡¥¨º¨¦??
String id = jTextField1.getText();
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
Book book = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().findById(
id);

if (book != null) {
jTextArea1.setText(book.toString());
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "This book does not exist", "message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "please enter ID", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// ¨¦?3yD??¡é
String id = jTextField1.getText();
boolean flag = false;
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().doDelete(
id);
if (!flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "This book does not exist", "message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "delete successful", "message", 1);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please fill in the book ID to be deleted", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText();
String name = jTextField8.getText();
String author = jTextField9.getText();
String classify = (String) jComboBox2.getSelectedItem();
String price = jTextField11.getText();
String publishdata = jTextField12.getText();
String news = jTextArea2.getText();
Book book = new Book();
book.setId(id);
book.setName(name);
book.setAuthor(author);
book.setClassify(classify);
book.setPrice(Double.parseDouble(price));
book.setNews(news);
book.setPublishdata(DateUtil.getStringToDate(publishdata));
boolean flag = false;
if(book!=null){
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().doUpdate(book);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "modification success", "message", 1);
}
else{
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "operating error", "message", 1);
}
}

}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String searchid = jTextField1.getText();
if (searchid != null && !searchid.equals("")) {
try {
Book book = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().findById(
searchid);
if (book != null) {
jLabel14.setText(String.valueOf(book.getId()));
jTextField3.setText(book.getName());
jTextField4.setText(book.getAuthor());
jComboBox1.setSelectedItem(book.getClassify());
jTextField6.setText(String.valueOf(book.getPrice()));
jTextField7.setText(String.valueOf(book.getPublishdata()));
jTextArea1.setText(book.getNews());
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The book you searched does not exist", "message", 1);
}

} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The book you searched does not exist", "message", 1);
}

}

private void jTextField1KeyPressed(java.awt.event.KeyEvent evt) {
// ?¨¬¨®|??3¦Ì?¨¹
if (evt.getKeyChar() == '\n') {
jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("searching...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<Borrow> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(
results, head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("searching done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);

new Thread() {
public void run() {
int i = 0;
while (i <= need_time) {
try {
Thread.sleep(1);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
}

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {

jProgressBar1.setValue(100);
jLabel2.setText("searching done");
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding information", "message", 1);
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
return;
}

}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("searching...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<Borrow> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(results,
head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("searching done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);

new Thread() {
public void run() {

try {

// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();

jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {
// ¨¨?1?2?¡ä??¨²...

}

private void jTextField1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// TODO add your handling code here:
}

private Object[][] getResult(List<Borrow> list) {
Object[][] results = new Object[list.size()][head.length];
for (int i = 0; i < list.size(); i++) {
Borrow borrow = list.get(i);
results[i][0] = borrow.getId();
results[i][1] = borrow.getReader_id();
results[i][2] = borrow.getBook_id();
results[i][3] = borrow.getBorrow_date();
results[i][4] = borrow.getBack_date();
results[i][5] = borrow.getIs_back();

}
return results;
}

private void jTextField3KeyPressed(java.awt.event.KeyEvent evt) {

if (evt.getKeyChar() == '\n') {
String reader_id = jTextField2.getText();
String borrow_date = jTextField3.getText();

if (reader_id == null || reader_id.equals("")
|| borrow_date.equals("") || borrow_date == null) {
JOptionPane
.showMessageDialog(this, "readers ID input errors or date format error!", "error", 0);
return;
}
Reader reader = new Reader();
try {
reader = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findById(
reader_id);
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (reader == null) {
JOptionPane
.showMessageDialog(this, "readers ID input errors or date format error!", "error", 0);
return;
}
int id = reader.getDays_num();
jLabel6.setText(DateUtil.getAfterDay(borrow_date, id));

}
}

private void jButton3ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// ??3yD??¡é
jTextField1.setText("");
jTextField2.setText("");
jTextField3.setText("");
jLabel6.setText("");
jTextField1.requestFocus();

}

dispose();
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
String book_id = jTextField1.getText().trim();
String reader_id = jTextField2.getText().trim();
String borrow_date = jTextField3.getText().trim();
String back_date = jLabel6.getText().trim();

Borrow borrow = new Borrow();
Reader reader = new Reader();
if (reader_id != null && !reader_id.equals("")) {
try {
reader = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findById(
reader_id);
if (reader != null) {
//?D??¨º?¡¤?¨®D?a???¨¢??
borrow.setBook_id(book_id);
borrow.setReader_id(reader_id);
borrow.setBorrow_date(DateUtil.getStringToDate(borrow_date));
borrow.setBack_date(DateUtil.getStringToDate(back_date));
borrow.setIs_back(1);
boolean flag = false;
{
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().doCreate(
borrow);
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Add successful",
"message", 1);

} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please input carefully!",
"message", 1);
}
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "readers ID input errors or date format error!",
"message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e1) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e1.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e1) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e1.printStackTrace();
}

} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please input carefully¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// 2¨¦?¡¥?¨¨??D??¡é
String id = jTextField1.getText();
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
Borrow borrow = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().findById(Integer.parseInt(id));

if (borrow != null) {
jTextArea1.setText(borrow.toString());
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "??¨®D??¨®|¦Ì??¨¨??D??¡é¡ê?", "???¡é", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, " Please enter your serial number", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// ¨¦?3yD??¡é
String id = jTextField1.getText();
boolean flag = false;
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().doDelete(
Integer.parseInt(id));
if (!flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding borrowing information!", "message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "deleted successfully", "message", 1);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please fill in the serial number to delete!", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String searchid = jTextField1.getText();
Borrow borrow = new Borrow();
Boolean flag = false;
if (searchid != null && !searchid.equals("")) {

try {
borrow = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().findById(searchid);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (borrow != null) {
borrow.setIs_back(0);
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().doUpdate(borrow);
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Return successfully¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Return failed¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please input the reader number¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String searchid = jTextField1.getText().trim();
String searchid2 = jTextField5.getText().trim();
Reader reader = new Reader();
Book book = new Book();
Borrow borrow = new Borrow();
if (searchid != null && !searchid.equals("") && searchid2 != null
&& !searchid2.equals("")) {

try {
reader = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findById(
searchid);
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (reader != null) {

try {

borrow = DAOFactory.getIBorrowDAOInstance().findById(
reader.getId());//2?¨ºyString
} catch (Exception e1) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e1.printStackTrace();
}

if (borrow != null) {

try {
book = DAOFactory.getIBookDAOInstance().findById(
searchid2);
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (book == null) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The book does not exist or has been canceled!", "message",
1);
return;
}
if (book != null && borrow != null) {

jLabel14.setText(String.valueOf(book.getId()));
jTextField3.setText(book.getName());
jTextField4.setText(book.getAuthor());
jComboBox1.setSelectedItem(book.getClassify());
jTextField6.setText(String.valueOf(book.getPrice()));
jTextField7.setText(String.valueOf(book
.getPublishdata()));
jTextArea1.setText(book.getNews());

jTextField8.setText(reader.getName());
jTextField12.setText(String.valueOf(borrow
.getBorrow_date()));
jTextField2.setText(String.valueOf(borrow
.getBack_date()));

//¨¦¨¨???aD?label???¨¢
jTextField3.setEditable(false);
jTextField4.setEditable(false);
jComboBox1.setEditable(false);
jTextField6.setEditable(false);
jTextField7.setEditable(false);
jTextArea1.setEditable(false);

jTextField8.setEditable(false);
jTextField12.setEditable(false);
jTextField2.setEditable(false);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding read information¡ê?", "message", 1);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The reader does not exist!", "message", 1);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please input carefully!", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jPasswordField1KeyTyped(java.awt.event.KeyEvent evt) {
if (evt.getKeyChar() == '\n') {
String name = jTextField1.getText();
String pass = String.valueOf(jPasswordField1.getPassword());
User user = null;


if (name.equals("") || name == null) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "User name is not allowed to be empty", "error", 0);
return;
}
try {
user = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().findById(name);
if (user != null) {
if (user.getPass() != null && user.getPass().equals(pass)) {

GlobalUser.LOGIN_USER = user; // ????¦Ì¡À?¡ã¨®??¡ì


Main.start();
this.dispose();
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "User name or password wrong!");
return;
}
}
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (user == null) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(this, "User name or password wrong!", "message", 0);
return;
}

}

}

while(true){
try {
Thread.sleep(13000);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
message.setText("Tip: in the file menu can open the Windows tool!");

Thread.sleep(13000);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
message.setText("Tip: management menu can modify the login password!");

try {
Thread.sleep(13000);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
message.setText("--Application by Java.");

try {
Thread.sleep(13000);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
message.setText("Cheng Zhang");

}

}
}.start();

private void jTextField1KeyPressed(java.awt.event.KeyEvent evt) {

if (evt.getKeyChar() == '\n') {
jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("?y?¨²2¨¦?¡¥...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<Reader> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(
results, head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { false,true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("searching done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);

new Thread() {
public void run() {
int i = 0;
while (i <= need_time) {
try {
Thread.sleep(1);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
}

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {

jProgressBar1.setValue(100);
jLabel2.setText("searching done");
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding information", "message", 1);
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
return;
}

}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("searching...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<Reader> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(results,
head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { false,true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("searching done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);

new Thread() {
public void run() {
int i = 0;
while (i <= need_time) {
try {
Thread.sleep(1);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
}

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {

jProgressBar1.setValue(100);
jLabel2.setText("searching done");
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding information", "message", 1);
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
return;
}

}

private void jTextField1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

}

private Object[][] getResult(List<Reader> list) {
Object[][] results = new Object[list.size()][head.length];
for (int i = 0; i < list.size(); i++) {
Reader reader = list.get(i);
results[i][0] = reader.getIncre_id();
results[i][1] = reader.getId();
results[i][2] = reader.getName();
results[i][3] = reader.getType();
results[i][4] = reader.getSex();
results[i][5] = reader.getDays_num();

}
return results;
}

}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText().trim();
String name = jTextField2.getText().trim();
String sex = (String) jComboBox2.getSelectedItem();
String type = (String) jComboBox3.getSelectedItem();
String days_num = jTextField5.getText().trim();

Reader reader = new Reader();
reader.setId(id);
reader.setName(name);
reader.setSex(sex);
reader.setType(type);
reader.setDays_num(Integer.parseInt(days_num));

User user = new User();
if (reader != null) {
user.setLogin_id(String.valueOf(reader.getId()));
user.setName(reader.getName());
user.setPass("12345");
user.setIs_admin(1);
}
boolean flag = false;
if (reader != null) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().doCreate(reader);
if (user != null) {
flag = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().doCreate(user);
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Add successful", "message", 1);

}
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
}

}

}

private void jButton3ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
this.dispose();

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText().trim();
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
Reader reader = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findById(
id);

if (reader != null) {
jTextArea1.setText(reader.toString());
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The reader does not exist!", "message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please enter your serial number", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText();
boolean flag = false;
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().doDelete(
id);
if (!flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The reader does not exist!", "message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Delete Successful", "message", 1);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please fill out to remove the reader number!", "message", 1);
}
}

new ReaderDelete().setVisible(true);
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jLabel14.getText();
String name = jTextField8.getText();
String sex = (String) jComboBox4.getSelectedItem();
String type = (String) jComboBox2.getSelectedItem();
int days_num = Integer.parseInt(jTextField4.getText());

if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {

Reader reader = new Reader();
reader.setId(id);
reader.setName(name);
reader.setSex(sex);
reader.setType(type);
reader.setDays_num(days_num);
boolean flag = false;
if (reader != null) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().doUpdate(reader);
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "modification success", "message", 1);
}
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
}
}else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The reader does not exit", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {
// 2¨¦?¡¥¨®??¡ì
String searchid = jTextField1.getText();
if (searchid != null && !searchid.equals("")) {
try {
Reader reader = DAOFactory.getIReaderDAOInstance().findById(
searchid);
if (reader != null) {
jLabel14.setText(String.valueOf(reader.getId()));
jTextField3.setText(reader.getName());
jComboBox3.setSelectedItem(reader.getSex());
jComboBox1.setSelectedItem(reader.getType());
jTextField2.setText(String.valueOf(reader.getDays_num()));

jTextField2.setEditable(false);
jTextField3.setEditable(false);
jComboBox3.setEditable(false);
jComboBox1.setEditable(false);
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The reader does not exit", "message", 1);
}

} catch (NumberFormatException e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {
// TODO Auto-generated catch block
e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The reader does not exit¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

}

private void jTextField1KeyPressed(java.awt.event.KeyEvent evt) {

if (evt.getKeyChar() == '\n') {
jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("searching...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<User> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(
results, head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("searching done");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);

new Thread() {
public void run() {
int i = 0;
while (i <= need_time) {
try {
Thread.sleep(1);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
}

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {

jProgressBar1.setValue(100);
jLabel2.setText("2¨¦?¡¥¨ª¨º3¨¦¡ê?");
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "There is no corresponding information¡ê?", "message", 1);
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
return;
}

}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

jProgressBar1.setVisible(true);


Long search_start = System.currentTimeMillis();
Long search_end = 0L;

jLabel2.setText("searching...");


String key_word = jTextField1.getText();
List<User> alllist = null;
try {
alllist = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().findAll(key_word);
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (alllist.size() != 0) {
Object[][] results = getResult(alllist);
jTable1.setModel(new javax.swing.table.DefaultTableModel(results,
head) {

private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
boolean[] canEdit = new boolean[] { true, true, true, true,
true, true, true };

public boolean isCellEditable(int rowIndex, int columnIndex) {
return canEdit[columnIndex];
}
});
jLabel2.setText("searching done¡ê?");


search_end = System.currentTimeMillis();
final int need_time = (int) (search_end - search_start);
jProgressBar1.setMaximum(need_time);


new Thread() {
public void run() {
int i = 0;
while (i <= need_time) {
try {
Thread.sleep(1);
} catch (InterruptedException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
jProgressBar1.setValue(i);
i++;
}
jProgressBar1.setVisible(false);
}

}.start();

}
if (alllist.size() == 0) {

jProgressBar1.setValue(100);
jLabel2.setText("searching done¡ê?");

}

}

private void jTextField1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

}

private Object[][] getResult(List<User> list) {
Object[][] results = new Object[list.size()][head.length];
for (int i = 0; i < list.size(); i++) {
User user = list.get(i);
results[i][0] = user.getId();
results[i][1] = user.getLogin_id();
results[i][2] = user.getPass();
results[i][3] = user.getName();
results[i][4] = user.getIs_admin();

}
return results;
}


public static void start() {
java.awt.EventQueue.invokeLater(new Runnable() {
public void run() {
new User_K_Find().setVisible(true);
}
});

}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String login_id = jTextField1.getText().trim();
String pass = jTextField2.getText().trim();
String name = jTextField3.getText().trim();
int is_admin = jComboBox1.getSelectedIndex();
boolean flag = false;

User user = new User();
if (login_id != null && !login_id.equals("") && pass != null
&& !pass.equals("")) {

user.setLogin_id(login_id);
user.setPass(pass);
user.setName(name);
user.setIs_admin(is_admin);
if (user != null) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().doCreate(user);
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Add successful", "message", 1);
}
else{
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Operation error or the user already exists!", "message", 1);
}
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please input carefully!", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText();
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
User user = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().findById(id);

if (user != null) {
jTextArea1.setText(user.toString());
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The user does not exist", "message", 1);
}
} catch (NumberFormatException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please enter your serial number", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText();
boolean flag = false;
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().doDelete(id);

} catch (NumberFormatException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Delete Successful", "message", 1);
}
if (!flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The user does not exist", "message", 1);
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "Please fill in the user number you want to delete!", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String id = jTextField1.getText();
if (id != null && !id.equals("")) {
try {
User user = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().findById(id);

if (user != null) {
jTextArea1.setText(user.toString());

e.printStackTrace();

e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "please enter the serial number", "message", 1);
}
}

private void jButton3ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

this.dispose();
}

private void jButton2ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String login_id = jLabel14.getText();
String name = jTextField8.getText();
String pass = jTextField4.getText();
int is_admin = jComboBox2.getSelectedIndex();

User user = new User();
user.setLogin_id(login_id);
user.setName(name);
user.setPass(pass);
user.setIs_admin(is_admin);
boolean flag = false;
if (user != null) {
try {
flag = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().doUpdate(user);
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
if (flag) {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "modification success¡ê?", "message", 1);
}else{
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "please fill it carefully", "message", 1);
}
}
}

private void jButton1ActionPerformed(java.awt.event.ActionEvent evt) {

String searchid = jTextField1.getText();
if (searchid != null && !searchid.equals("")) {
try {
User user = DAOFactory.getIUserDAOInstance().findById(
(searchid));
if (user != null) {
jLabel14.setText(String.valueOf(user.getLogin_id()));
jTextField3.setText(user.getName());
jTextField2.setText(user.getPass());
jComboBox1.setSelectedIndex(user.getIs_admin());

jTextField3.setEditable(false);
jTextField2.setEditable(false);
jComboBox1.setEditable(false);
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The user does not exist¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

} catch (NumberFormatException e) {

e.printStackTrace();
} catch (Exception e) {

e.printStackTrace();
}
} else {
JOptionPane.showMessageDialog(null, "The user does not exist¡ê?", "message", 1);
}

}

MySQL Database script

DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS _library;
CREATE DATABASE _library;
USE _library;
--
--
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS library_book;
CREATE TABLE library_book(
incre_id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
id VARCHAR(60) unique NOT NULL,
name VARCHAR(60) NOT NULL,
author VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
classify VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
price DOUBLE NOT NULL,
news VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
publishdata DATE
);
--
--
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS library_reader;
CREATE TABLE library_reader(
incre_id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
id VARCHAR(60) NOT NULL UNIQUE ,
name varchar(50) not null ,
type varchar(20) not null,
sex varchar(2) not null,
days_num int(11)
);

--
--
--
--
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS library_borrow;
CREATE TABLE library_borrow(
id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
reader_id varchar(50) not null ,
book_id varchar(50) not null ,
borrow_date date not null,
back_date date not null,
is_back int(1) not null
);
--
--
--
--
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS library_user;
CREATE TABLE library_user(
id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
login_id varchar(50) NOT NULL unique ,
name varchar(50),
pass varchar(50) not null,
is_admin int(1)
);
CREATE INDEX borrow_index ON library_borrow (reader_id);
CREATE INDEX book_index ON library_book (id);
CREATE INDEX reader_index ON library_reader (id);
CREATE INDEX user_index ON library_user (login_id);

--
--
--
insert into library_user (login_id,name,pass,is_admin) values('admin','admin','admin',0);
